<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pickle&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pickle&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈpɪkl̩/</span></li>
<li><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r50165410">.mw-parser-output .k-player .k-attribution{visibility:hidden}</style><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: bottom; display:inline-block; list-style:none;line-height: 1em; border-collapse:collapse;"><tbody><tr><td class="unicode audiolink" style="padding-right:5px; padding-left: 0;">Audio (AU)</td><td class="audiofile"><span class="mw-tmh-player audio" style="width:175px;"><audio id="mwe_player_0_placeholder" preload="none" width="175" style="width:175px;" data-durationhint="1" data-mwtitle="En-au-pickle.ogg" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons" disabled="disabled" tabindex="-1"></audio><a class="mw-tmh-play" href="/wiki/File:En-au-pickle.ogg" title="Play media" role="button"><span class="mw-tmh-play-icon"></span></a><span class="mw-tmh-duration mw-tmh-label" aria-label="1 second">0:01</span></span></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:En-au-pickle.ogg" title="File:En-au-pickle.ogg">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></li>
<li>Rhymes: <a href="/wiki/Rhymes:English/%C9%AAk%C9%99l" title="Rhymes:English/ɪkəl"><span class="IPA">-ɪkəl</span></a></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pickle&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/pikel#Middle_English" title="pikel">pikel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spicy sauce served with meat or fish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href="/wiki/pekel#Middle_Low_German" title="pekel">pekel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">brine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href="/wiki/pikkill#Scots" title="pikkill">pikkill</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">salt liquor, brine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq"><a href="/wiki/Piekele#Saterland_Frisian" title="Piekele">Piekele</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pickle, brine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/pekel#Dutch" title="pekel">pekel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pickle, brine</span><span <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pickle&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/w/index.php?title=pickel&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="pickel (page does not exist)">pickel</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete and rare</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pickle&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:CucumberDillPickles.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/CucumberDillPickles.jpg/220px-CucumberDillPickles.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="330" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/CucumberDillPickles.jpg/330px-CucumberDillPickles.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/CucumberDillPickles.jpg/440px-CucumberDillPickles.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2592" data-file-height="3888"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:CucumberDillPickles.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>a jar of pickles</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">pickle</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pickles#English" title="pickles">pickles</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href="/wiki/cucumber" title="cucumber">cucumber</a> preserved in a <a href="/wiki/solution" title="solution">solution</a>, usually a <a href="/wiki/brine" title="brine">brine</a> or a <a href="/wiki/vinegar" title="vinegar">vinegar</a> syrup.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">A <b>pickle</b> goes well with a hamburger.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often in the <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#plural" title="Appendix:Glossary">plural</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any vegetable preserved in vinegar and consumed as <a href="/wiki/relish" title="relish">relish</a>.</li>
<li>A sweet, vinegary pickled <a href="/wiki/chutney" title="chutney">chutney</a> popular in <a href="/wiki/Britain" title="Britain">Britain</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/brine" title="brine">brine</a> used for preserving food.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">This tub is filled with the <b>pickle</b> that we will put the small cucumbers into.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#informal" title="Appendix:Glossary">informal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A difficult situation; <a href="/wiki/peril" title="peril">peril</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonym&nbsp;▲</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:difficult_situation" title="Thesaurus:difficult situation">Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">difficult situation</span></a></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The climber found himself in a <b>pickle</b> when one of the rocks broke off.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1955</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rex_Stout" class="extiw" title="w:Rex Stout">Rex Stout</a>, "Die Like a Dog", in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Three_Witnesses_(book)" class="extiw" title="w:Three Witnesses (book)"><i>Three Witnesses</i></a>, October 1994 <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bantam_Books" class="extiw" title="w:Bantam Books">Bantam</a> edition, <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0553249592" title="Special:BookSources/0553249592">→ISBN</a>, page 194:
<dl><dd>I beg you, Miss Jones, to realize the <b>pickle</b> you're in.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/endearing" title="endearing">endearing</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mildly <a href="/wiki/mischievous" title="mischievous">mischievous</a> <a href="/wiki/loved_one" title="loved one">loved one</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1867</b>,  Polly Stubbs,  <cite>Nursery times; or, Stories about the little ones, by an old nurse</cite>, page 143:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">by degrees my little <b>pickle</b> (who, as I told you at the beginning of the story, was the most troublesome child I ever came across) turned into a very well-behaved young gentleman.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1885</b>,  Eleanor A. Bulley,  <cite>Great Britain for little Britons</cite>, page 116:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">... If you could get my little <b>pickle</b> to learn his multiplication table before you leave us, you shall have that musical box to take home with you.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1965</b>,  Eric Malpass,  <cite>Morning's at seven</cite>, page 43:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">'And now,' she said, 'what about that kiss my little <b>pickle</b> was going to give his old Auntie?'</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/baseball" title="baseball">baseball</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/rundown" title="rundown">rundown</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Jones was caught in a <b>pickle</b> between second and third.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A children’s game with three participants that emulates a baseball <a href="/wiki/rundown" title="rundown">rundown</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The boys played <b>pickle</b> in the front yard for an hour.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/penis" title="penis">penis</a>.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonym&nbsp;▲</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:penis" title="Thesaurus:penis">Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">penis</span></a></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pipe for smoking <a href="/wiki/methamphetamine" title="methamphetamine">methamphetamine</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Load some shards in that <b>pickle</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metalworking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/bath" title="bath">bath</a> of <a href="/wiki/dilute" title="dilute">dilute</a> sulphuric or nitric acid, etc., to remove burnt sand, scale, rust, etc., from the surface of <a href="/wiki/casting" title="casting">castings</a>, or other articles of metal, or to brighten them or improve their colour.</li>
<li>In an <a href="/w/index.php?title=optical_landing_system&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="optical landing system (page does not exist)">optical landing system</a>, the hand-held <a href="/wiki/controller" title="controller">controller</a> connected to the <a href="/wiki/lens" title="lens">lens</a>, or <a href="/wiki/apparatus" title="apparatus">apparatus</a> on which the <a href="/wiki/light" title="light">lights</a> are mounted.</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/piccalilli#English" title="piccalilli">piccalilli</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pickle&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">pickle</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pickles#English" title="pickles">pickles</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pickling#English" title="pickling">pickling</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pickled#English" title="pickled">pickled</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#ergative" title="Appendix:Glossary">ergative</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/preserve" title="preserve">preserve</a> food (or sometimes other things) in a <a href="/wiki/salt" title="salt">salt</a>, <a href="/wiki/sugar" title="sugar">sugar</a> or <a href="/wiki/vinegar" title="vinegar">vinegar</a> solution.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">We <b>pickled</b> the remainder of the crop.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">These cucumbers <b>pickle</b> very well.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><span class="see-cites">For more quotations using this term, see <a href="/wiki/Citations:pickle#English" title="Citations:pickle">Citations:pickle</a>.</span></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To remove high-temperature <a href="/wiki/scale" title="scale">scale</a> and <a href="/wiki/oxidation" title="oxidation">oxidation</a> from metal with heated (often sulphuric) industrial <a href="/wiki/acid" title="acid">acid</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The crew will <b>pickle</b> the fittings in the morning.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/programming#Noun" title="programming">programming</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> in <a href="/wiki/Python" title="Python">Python</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/serialize" title="serialize">serialize</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>2005</b>, Peter Norton <i>et al</i>, <i>Beginning Python</i>:
<dl><dd>You can now restore the <b>pickled</b> data. If you like, close your Python interpreter and open a new instance, to convince yourself <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b>,  Marty Alchin,  <cite>Pro Django</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">To illustrate how this would work in practice, consider a field designed to store and retrieve a <b>pickled</b> copy of any arbitrary Python object.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#historical" title="Appendix:Glossary">historical</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To pour <a href="/wiki/brine" title="brine">brine</a> over a person after flogging them, as a method of punishment.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1756</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Thistlewood" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Thomas Thistlewood">Thomas Thistlewood</a>, diary, quoted in <b>2001</b>, Glyne A. Griffith, <i>Caribbean Cultural Identities</i>, Bucknell University Press (<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9780838754757" title="Special:BookSources/9780838754757">→ISBN</a>), page 38:
<dl><dd>On Wednesday 26 May, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> I had [an enslaved man] flogged and <b>pickled</b> and then made Hector shit in his mouth. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> In July, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> Gave [another enslaved man] a moderate whipping, <b>pickled</b> him well, made Hector shit in his mouth, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2016</b>, Christopher P. Magra, <i>Poseidon's Curse: British Naval Impressment and Atlantic Origins of the American Revolution</i>, Cambridge University Press (<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9781316875919" title="Special:BookSources/9781316875919">→ISBN</a>), page 70:
<dl><dd>Naval seamen could also be keel-hauled, ducked, <b>pickled</b>, and flogged around the fleet.
<dl><dd>[elsewhere, page 93, the book explains:] A <b>pickled</b> man had his flogged back washed with vinegar.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pickle&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from Scottish <a href="#Scottish">pickle</a>, apparently from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pick#English" title="pick">pick</a></i> +‎ <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/-le#English" title="-le">-le</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">diminutive suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href="/w/index.php?title=pickil&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="pickil (page does not exist)">pickil</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pickle&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">pickle</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pickles#English" title="pickles">pickles</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_England" class="extiw" title="w:Northern England">Northern England</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/kernel" title="kernel">kernel</a>; a <a href="/wiki/grain" title="grain">grain</a> (of salt, sugar, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_England" class="extiw" title="w:Northern England">Northern England</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A small or indefinite quantity or amount (of something); a little, a bit, a few. Usually in <a href="/wiki/partitive" title="partitive">partitive</a> construction, frequently without "of"; a single grain or kernel of wheat, barley, oats, sand or dust.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1881</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Louis_Stevenson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robert Louis Stevenson">Robert Louis Stevenson</a>, "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thrawn_Janet" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Thrawn Janet">Thrawn Janet</a>"
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> ill things are like guid—they baith come bit by bit, a <b>pickle</b> at a time <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pickle&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">pickle</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pickles#English" title="pickles">pickles</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pickling#English" title="pickling">pickling</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pickled#English" title="pickled">pickled</a></b>)
</p>
